      <ir-faq-hub _ngcontent-c102="" _nghost-c49="">
       <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="contain">
        <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__content">
         <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__header">
          <h4 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h2">
           <!---->FAQ</h4>
          <!---->
          <!---->
          <!---->
          <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__header--button">
           <a _ngcontent-c49="" class="button--secondary" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" href="https://www.udacity.com/design-sprint/faq">View All FAQ</a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="more fade">
          <div _ngcontent-c49="">
           <!---->
           <ul _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__list">
            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">Program Highlight</h5>
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Why should I enroll in the Design Sprint Foundations Nanodegree program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="The ability to efficiently and effectively problem solve is an invaluable skill in virtually any field, and it&amp;#8217;s invaluable at both an individual and organizational level. Today&amp;#8217;s technologically-powered economy rewards rapid innovation, and the best companies in the world are using the revolutionary design sprint process to create, prototype, test, and release new products, as well as develop new strategies, enter new markets, and more. In this program, you&amp;#8217;ll learn exactly how and why the design sprint process is so effective, and why it&amp;#8217;s become so integral to the success of so many leading companies. You&amp;#8217;ll learn how a design sprint works, how to participate in one, and how to lead one yourself. To ensure you&amp;#8217;re learning from the best, we&amp;#8217;ve partnered with international design firm AJ&amp;amp;Smart, who have pioneered a Version 2.0 of this influential process to design products for Lufthansa, Zalando, Red Bull, and more. Together, we&amp;#8217;ve built a hands-on learning experience that will enable you to master the design sprint process, and become an exceptional problem-solver with the skill to efficiently and effectively drive positive change in virtually any arena.">
              The ability to efficiently and effectively problem solve is an invaluable skill in virtually any field, and its invaluable at both an individual and organizational level. Todays technologically-powered economy rewards rapid innovation, and the best companies in the world are using the revolutionary design sprint process to create, prototype, test, and release new products, as well as develop new strategies, enter new markets, and more. In this program, youll learn exactly how and why the design sprint process is so effective, and why its become so integral to the success of so many leading companies. Youll learn how a design sprint works, how to participate in one, and how to lead one yourself. To ensure youre learning from the best, weve partnered with international design firm AJ&amp;Smart, who have pioneered a Version 2.0 of this influential process to design products for Lufthansa, Zalando, Red Bull, and more. Together, weve built a hands-on learning experience that will enable you to master the design sprint process, and become an exceptional problem-solver with the skill to efficiently and effectively drive positive change in virtually any arena.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What kinds of topics will the program cover?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="We will cover every topic necessary for you to be able to successfully participate in design sprints, and run them yourselves. You&amp;#8217;ll learn why design sprints work, how they work, and you&amp;#8217;ll experience the process yourself. The projects you build over the course of the program will simulate the actual experience of participating in, and contributing to, a real design sprint. You&amp;#8217;ll learn every aspect of the design sprint process at the hands-on level. Program topics include: supplies, challenges &amp;amp; sketching, deciding/voting, storyboarding, prototyping, and user-testing. You will also learn best practices for writing a summary report to implement your test results for future work.">
              We will cover every topic necessary for you to be able to successfully participate in design sprints, and run them yourselves. Youll learn why design sprints work, how they work, and youll experience the process yourself. The projects you build over the course of the program will simulate the actual experience of participating in, and contributing to, a real design sprint. Youll learn every aspect of the design sprint process at the hands-on level. Program topics include: supplies, challenges &amp; sketching, deciding/voting, storyboarding, prototyping, and user-testing. You will also learn best practices for writing a summary report to implement your test results for future work.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Will we have the opportunity to test out what we are learning in real-world environments?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Yes! For this program we have created a simulated design sprint experience based on a real-life problem that a fictitious business (created for this program) needs to solve. This simulated design sprint experience is led by our Udacity team, and our experts from AJ&amp;amp;Smart. You&amp;#8217;ll learn what happens on each day of a design sprint, and understand the responsibilities of each participant&amp;#8217;s role. You'll participate in each step of the process to help this company solve their challenges, and make actual contributions to the process through your project submissions! Actively engaging in all aspects of the design sprint process, with the support of expert instructors and moderators, is the best way to master this methodology. You'll gain a thorough and complete understanding of how the design process works, what it makes possible, and why it's such an effective strategy.">
              Yes! For this program we have created a simulated design sprint experience based on a real-life problem that a fictitious business (created for this program) needs to solve. This simulated design sprint experience is led by our Udacity team, and our experts from AJ&amp;Smart. Youll learn what happens on each day of a design sprint, and understand the responsibilities of each participants role. You'll participate in each step of the process to help this company solve their challenges, and make actual contributions to the process through your project submissions! Actively engaging in all aspects of the design sprint process, with the support of expert instructors and moderators, is the best way to master this methodology. You'll gain a thorough and complete understanding of how the design process works, what it makes possible, and why it's such an effective strategy.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Who is AJ&amp;Smart, and how are they involved?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="AJ&amp;amp;Smart is an international design agency that works with the best companies in the world to reshape their problem-solving processes. They have pioneered a cutting-edge version of the Design Sprint process popularized by Jake Knapp&amp;#8217;s New York Times bestseller &amp;#8220;Sprint,&amp;#8221; which they&amp;#8217;ve used to successfully design products for Lufthansa, Zalando, Red Bull, and more. AJ&amp;amp;Smart Instructors use instructional videos, quizzes, and projects to teach you everything you need to know about the design sprint process. Their expertise is felt throughout the program, and you&amp;#8217;ll actually see them on camera in some of your classroom videos. Please visit the <a href=&quot;https://www.http://ajsmart.com/&quot;>AJ&amp;amp;Smart website</a> for additional details.">
              AJ&amp;Smart is an international design agency that works with the best companies in the world to reshape their problem-solving processes. They have pioneered a cutting-edge version of the Design Sprint process popularized by Jake Knapps New York Times bestseller Sprint, which theyve used to successfully design products for Lufthansa, Zalando, Red Bull, and more. AJ&amp;Smart Instructors use instructional videos, quizzes, and projects to teach you everything you need to know about the design sprint process. Their expertise is felt throughout the program, and youll actually see them on camera in some of your classroom videos. Please visit the 
              <a href="https://www.http://ajsmart.com/">AJ&amp;Smart website</a> for additional details.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What is a Foundations Nanodegree program, and how does this differ from your existing Nanodegree programs?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="A Foundations Nanodegree program is designed to support focus on a particular area of learning. Depending on your longer-term goals, a Foundations Nanodegree program enables you to sample new areas of learning, enhance an existing skill set, or prepare for a career move that requires a fuller understanding of certain technologies and concepts. In the case of this program, the Design Sprint is a creative problem-solving tool, and considered an &amp;#8220;additive&amp;#8221; skill that layers in a key competitive differentiator to your existing skill set.">
              A Foundations Nanodegree program is designed to support focus on a particular area of learning. Depending on your longer-term goals, a Foundations Nanodegree program enables you to sample new areas of learning, enhance an existing skill set, or prepare for a career move that requires a fuller understanding of certain technologies and concepts. In the case of this program, the Design Sprint is a creative problem-solving tool, and considered an additive skill that layers in a key competitive differentiator to your existing skill set.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What jobs will this program prepare me for?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="As a Foundations Nanodegree program, the focus of the curriculum is not job-readiness. The skills you learn can certainly be very valuable in your job and career, but this program does not provide any career support or preparation.">
              As a Foundations Nanodegree program, the focus of the curriculum is not job-readiness. The skills you learn can certainly be very valuable in your job and career, but this program does not provide any career support or preparation.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Will I receive a credential when I graduate, as with other Nanodegree programs?</h6>

              Yes! You will receive a Design Sprint Foundations Nanodegree program credential after you successfully complete the program.

              It is not. The Design Sprint Foundations Nanodegree program is a one-month program that requires students to keep pace with their peers throughout the duration of the program.               No. Due to the fixed-term nature of the Design Sprint Foundations Nanodegree program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, it will not be possible to pause your enrollment in this program.

            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">Deadline Policy</h5>
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What is the program's deadline policy?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="When we use the term &amp;#34;deadline&amp;#34; with regards to Nanodegree program projects, we use it in one of two ways:&amp;#10;&amp;#10;A final deadline for passing all projects&amp;#10;Ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects&amp;#10;&amp;#10;It is very important to understand the distinctions between the two, as your progress in the program is measured against the deadlines we've established. Please see below for an explanation of what each usage means.&amp;#10;&amp;#10;A final deadline for passing all projects&amp;#10;Passing a project in this context means that a Udacity Reviewer has marked your project as &amp;#34;Meets Specifications.&amp;#34; In order to graduate, you have to pass all projects by the last day of your content access.&amp;#10;&amp;#10;Ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects&amp;#10;The deadlines you see in your classroom are suggestions for when you should ideally pass each project. They are meant to help keep you on track so that you maintain an appropriate pace throughout the program, and graduate on time.">
              When we use the term "deadline" with regards to Nanodegree program projects, we use it in one of two ways: A final deadline for passing all projects Ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects It is very important to understand the distinctions between the two, as your progress in the program is measured against the deadlines we've established. Please see below for an explanation of what each usage means. A final deadline for passing all projects Passing a project in this context means that a Udacity Reviewer has marked your project as "Meets Specifications." In order to graduate, you have to pass all projects by the last day of your content access. Ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects The deadlines you see in your classroom are suggestions for when you should ideally pass each project. They are meant to help keep you on track so that you maintain an appropriate pace throughout the program, and graduate on time.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What happens if I don't complete a Nanodegree program project on time?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="It is strongly recommended that you complete each project on time to ensure you meet graduation requirements. If you do not pass all the required Nanodegree program projects by the last day of your term, you will lose access to the program and content. See Deadline Policy above.">
              It is strongly recommended that you complete each project on time to ensure you meet graduation requirements. If you do not pass all the required Nanodegree program projects by the last day of your term, you will lose access to the program and content. See Deadline Policy above.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What are my options if I don't complete the Nanodegree program by the end of the term?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="If you do not complete the term by the term deadline, you will receive one free four-week extension, which will be automatically applied to your account. If you do not complete the term within the extension period, you will be removed from the program and will no longer be able to access course content. To resume access to the course, you would need to re-enroll in a new term and pay the associated enrollment fees again. Your progress will carry over, and you&amp;#8217;ll be able to resume where you left off.">
              If you do not complete the term by the term deadline, you will receive one free four-week extension, which will be automatically applied to your account. If you do not complete the term within the extension period, you will be removed from the program and will no longer be able to access course content. To resume access to the course, you would need to re-enroll in a new term and pay the associated enrollment fees again. Your progress will carry over, and youll be able to resume where you left off.
             </div></li>
